=head1 NAME

Locale::RecodeData::BIG_5

=head1 SYNOPSIS

This module is internal to libintl.  Do not use directly!

=head1 DESCRIPTION

The base for this module is generated and contains the conversion 
tables and routines for BIG_5.

BIG_5 is a multi-byte encoding!


=head1 COMMENTS

The following comments have been extracted from the original charmap:


 Chinese charmap for BIG_5 (CP950)
 version: 0.92
 Contact: Tung-Han Hsieh   E<lt>thhsieh@linux.org.twE<gt>
	   Yuan-Chung Cheng E<lt>platin@ms31.hinet.netE<gt>
 Distribution and use is free, even for comercial purpose.

 This charmap is converted from:
     ftp://ftp.unicode.org/Public/MAPPINGS/VENDORS/MICSFT/WINDOWS/CP950.TXT
 and also merged several characters (/xc6/xa1-/xc7/xfc) from:
     Aprhic Tech. CO., LTD. Big5 E<lt>==E<gt> Unicode mapping table.

 Irrevsible mapping Big5 characters (using %IRREVERSIBLE% notation):
     /xa2/xcc, /xa2/xce, /xf9/xe9, /xf9/xea, /xf9/xeb, 
     /xf9/xf9, /xf9/xfa, /xf9/xfb, /xf9/xfc, /xf9/xfd

 alias BIG_5-CP950

Please note that aliases listed above are not necessarily valid!

=head1 CHARACTER TABLE

The following table is sorted in the same order as the original charmap.
All character codes are in hexadecimal.  Please read 'Unicode' as
'ISO-10646-UCS4'.

       Local |  Unicode | Description
-------------+----------+-----------------------------------------------

         /x00 | 00000000 | NULL (NUL)
         /x01 | 00000001 | START OF HEADING (SOH)
         /x02 | 00000002 | START OF TEXT (STX)
         /x03 | 00000003 | END OF TEXT (ETX)
         /x04 | 00000004 | END OF TRANSMISSION (EOT)
         /x05 | 00000005 | ENQUIRY (ENQ)
         /x06 | 00000006 | ACKNOWLEDGE (ACK)
         /x07 | 00000007 | BELL (BEL)
         /x08 | 00000008 | BACKSPACE (BS)
